\centerline{\Large\bf Abstract} \vskip 6mm \songti\zihao{-4}
%\vskip 0.5mm\centerline{\Large\bf Abstract}\vskip 0.5cm
\label{pg:ii}
\par

Nowadays, the inventory problem is a classical and significant issue in the Operations Research literature. 
Decision making in inventory problem is always accompanied by uncertainty especially when dealing with demands of new products, fashion goods and other seasonal products. 
The uncertainty usually brings the risk of losses. Therefore, if we know how to deal with the risk of losses correctly, we can make rational policies for the inventory problem.
In the classical modeling approach, an optimal inventory policy has to trade off the risk and the total expected profit 
with further consideration on the decision makers' declared risk preference. In the decision-making process, 
the risk neutral decision makers concern more about the profit of the products. 
However, risk averse decision makers in the inventory problem tend to be more concerned about the risk of losses compared with profit. 
Therefore, in this dissertation, we study the profit and risk of the multi-item single-period inventory problem from two aspects: risk neutral and risk aversion.

This dissertation mainly studies the risk-neutral and risk-averse multi-item single-period inventory problem by credibility optimization method in fuzzy environment. 
Firstly, the risk-neutral multi-item inventory model is established, the goal of proposed model is to maximize the profit. 
Secondly, when the uncertain demands are mutually independent fuzzy variables, we analyze the properties of the proposed model and discuss the solution method.  
Furthermore, this dissertation considers profit and risk simultaneously, and establishes the risk-averse absolute semi-deviation inventory models by using the multi-objective method. 
Then we transform the bi-objective model into its equivalent single-onjective forms and give the model analysis by the min-max modeling idea.
Subsequently, we give the calculating formulas of the absolute semi-deviation for the reciprocal of the demand undercommon possibility distributions.
Finally, the numerical experiment for the equivalent models is given, and the results demonstrate the effectiveness of the modeling idea and the solution method.

The major contribution of this dissertation includes the following four aspects:
(i) Risk-neutral and risk-averse multi-item inventory models are built;
(ii) The equivalent models of the expected value and the absolute semi-deviation inventory problem are analyzed respectively in fuzzy environment;
(iii) This dissertation discusses the properties of the uncertain demand under common fixed possibility distributions and variable possibility distributions 
and presents the theoretical results;
(iv) The numerical experiments are designed for the three classes of inventory models and the results are obtained by softwares, 
which illustrate the modeling ideas and demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed optimization methods.
 
\medskip

\smallskip

 {\CC Ht >v 2{\char95} VF 6( U{\char95} Ok R* ;q 5C Wn 4s {\char64}{\char123} Hs~{\char35},\CCA  K{\char123} CG M( 3{\char35} SC {\char64}{\char123} Hs 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 Ww N* D? 1j :/ J{\char125} 2{\char34} Wn 4s ;/ W{\char92} F= >y {\char64}{\char123}Hs
~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC :{\char92} H] RW 5C 5= 5{\char37} 2z F7 5D ?b 4f D{\char35} PM~{\char35},\CCA  Fd {\char64}{\char123} Hs D? 1j :/ J{\char125} N*
} \[
\pi(x,\xi)=px-a-\frac{h{x}^{2}}{2\xi},
\]
 {\CC Fd VP} $px$  {\CC N* ?b 4f NJ Lb VP 5D W{\char92} JU Rf~{\char35},} \CCA $a$  {\CC N* 9L 6( 6) 9: 3I 1>~{\char35},} \CCA $hx^{2}/2\xi$  {\CC N* ?b 4f 3I 1>~{\char35}.\CCA
 D{\char35} :{\char125} {\char64}{\char123} Hs} $\pi(x,\xi)$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 SI} $\mathrm{E}[\pi(x,\xi)]$ {\CC 1m J>~{\char35}.\CCA  SI ND OW} \cite{Liu2002} {\CC VP 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 Kc WS 5D PT VJ ?I V*
} \begin{equation}\label{equation1}
\begin{split}
\E[\pi(x,\xi)]&=\mathrm{E}\left[px-a-\frac{h{x}^{2}}{2\xi}\right]\\
&=px-a-\E\left[\frac{h{x}^{2}}{2\xi}\right]\\
&=px-a-\frac{h{x}^{2}}{2}\E\left[\frac{1}{\xi}\right].\\
\end{split}
\end{equation}

 {\CC TZ Ub VV Gi PN OB~{\char35},\CCA  5{\char37} 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ ?b 4f NJ Lb 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 D{\char35} PM N*
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{ex-model--1}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\max \quad \mathrm{E}[\pi(x,\xi)]\\
&{\rm s.\; t.}\quad x\geq 0.\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}

 {\CC 8y >] 9+ J=} (\ref{equation1}), {\CC ?I 5C 5= D{\char35} PM} (\ref{ex-model--1}) {\CC 5D =b~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
x^{\ast}=\frac{p}{hm},
\]
 {\CC Fd VP} $m=\E[1/\xi]$.

 {\CC TZ OV J5 Iz ;n VP~{\char35},\CCA  6` 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ ?b 4f NJ Lb TZ {\char64}m B[ :M J5 <J S{\char38} SC 7= Cf 8{\char124} >{\char95} VX R* Rb Re~{\char35}.\CCA  =S OB {\char64}4 ND UB =+ LV B[ 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ DZ 2; M, 2z F75D
 ?b 4f NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA
 An} $i=1,2,\ldots,n$  {\CC 1m J> 2z F7 5D {\char64}` PM 2{\char34} <Y Ih HN Rb A= VV 2z F7 V. <d C; SP O` ;{\char37} S0 Ol~{\char35}.\CCA  Ub Qy~{\char35},\CCA  6` 2z F7 {\char64}{\char123} Hs :/ J{\char125} <4 ?I 1m J> N*
} \[
\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})=\sum_{i=1}^{n}\left(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2\xi_{i}}\right).
\]

 {\CC TZ 7g OU VP A{\char34} 5D W< Tr OB~{\char35},\CCA  6` 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ ?b 4f NJ Lb 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 D{\char35} PM 99 =( Hg OB~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model--3}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\max \quad \E[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]\\
&{\rm s.\; t.}\quad \textbf{x}\geq 0.\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}

 {\CC Ht <G Ph Gs Or A? N*} $\bm{\xi}$ {\CC GR} $\bm{\xi}=(\xi_{1},\xi_{2},\cdots,\xi_{n})$, {\CC 2{\char34} <Y Ih Ph Gs 1d A?} $\xi_i$  {\CC JG O` ;{\char37} 6{\char64} A{\char34} 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} \cite{LiuGao2007}, {\CC Tr A* :O ?I D{\char92}PT
 7V 2<} $\mu_{\bm{\xi}}$  {\CC P4 Ww
} $$
\mu_{\bm{\xi}}(t_{1},t_{2},\cdots,t_{n})=\min_{1\leq i\leq n}\mu_{\xi_{i}}(t_{i}).
$$
 {\CC An
} \[
\pi_{i}(x_i,\xi_{i})=p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2\xi_{i}}, \quad i=1,2,\ldots,n.
\]
 {\CC Tr } $\pi_{i}(x_i,\xi_{i}),i=1,2,\ldots,n$,  {\CC R2 JG O` ;{\char37} 6{\char64} A{\char34} 5D~{\char35}.\CCA  SI FZ M{\char123} V5 Kc WS} \cite{Liu2003} {\CC 5D 6{\char64} A{\char34} O{\char95} PT ?I V*
} \[

\]
 {\CC <F Kc ?I 5C
} \[
\mathrm{E}[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]=\sum_{i=1}^{n}\left(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\mathrm{E}\left[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\right]\right).
\]
 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},\CCA  D{\char35} PM} (\ref{model--3}) {\CC 5D 5H <[ D{\char35} PM N*
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model--4}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\max \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{m_{i}h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\right)\\
&{\rm s.\; t.}\quad \textbf{x}\geq 0,\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
\noindent
 {\CC Fd VP
} \[
m_{i}=\E\left[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\right],\quad i=1,2,\ldots,n.
\]

 {\CC OT H;~{\char35},\CCA  D{\char35} PM} (\ref{model--4}) {\CC JG R; 8v M9 9f ;. D{\char35} PM~{\char35},\CCA  M( 9{\char125} Gs =b RT OB 7= 3L
} \[

\]
 {\CC ?I 5C
} \[
\textbf{x}^{\ast}=\left[\frac{p_{1}}{h_{1}m_{1}},\frac{p_{2}}{h_{2}m_{2}},\ldots,\frac{p_{n}}{h_{n}m_{n}}\right].
\]

 {\CC D? G0 N* V9~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG RQ >- 5C 5= AK D{\char35} PM} (\ref{model--4}) {\CC 5D R; 0c =b} $\textbf{x}^{\ast}$, {\CC Fd R{\char64} {\char64}5 SZ} $m_i=\E[{1}/{\xi_{i}}], i=1,2,\ldots,n$.
 {\CC OB R; =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG =+ LV B[ TZ 3{\char35} <{\char123} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB} $m_{i}, i=1,2,\ldots,n$  {\CC 5D <F Kc NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA

\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC 3{\char35} <{\char123} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D FZ M{\char123} V5
} \label{pg:2.2}}\hskip\parindent 
 {\CC TZ Ub R; =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG =+ TZ 3{\char35} <{\char123} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB LV B[ FZ M{\char123} V5} $\mathrm{E}[{1}/{\xi_{i}}]\,(i=1,2,\ldots,n)$  {\CC 5D <F Kc NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA
 7V 1p LV B[ A= VV Gi PN~{\char35},\CCA  R; VV JG Ph Gs} $\xi_{i}\,(i=1,2,\ldots,n)$  {\CC 7{\char126} 4S {\char64}k I{\char34} 7V 2<~{\char35},\CCA  Am R; VV JG Ph Gs 7{\char126} 4S 3{\char35} <{\char123} 5D A, Px 7V 2<~{\char35}.\CCA
} \subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC {\char64}k I{\char34} D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D FZ M{\char123} V5}} 
\label{pg:2.2.1} \hskip\parindent
\begin{theorem}\label{theorem2-1}
 {\CC <Y Ih D{\char35} PM} (\ref{ex-model--1}) {\CC VP 5D Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC 7{\char126} 4S RT OB {\char64}k I{\char34} 7V 2<

\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC Fd VP 6T HN Rb 5D} $i$, {\CC SP } $t_{i}\geq t_{i+1}$, $\mu_{i}>0$  {\CC GR } $\max_{1\leq i< +\infty}\mu_{i}=1$. {\CC Tr FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC N*

\end{equation}
 {\CC 6T SZ HN Rb 5D} $i$, {\CC SP } $\mu_0=0$.
\\\em \pf
 {\CC SI <Y Ih ?I V*~{\char35},\CCA  Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< Hg OB Ky J>

\begin{theorem}\label{theorem2-2}
 {\CC Hg 9{\char123} D{\char35} PM} (\ref{ex-model--1}) {\CC VP 5D Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3})$  {\CC GR } $r_{1}> 0$, {\CC Tr FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC N*

 {\CC TZ } $r_{1}=0$  {\CC 5D Gi ?v OB~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA
} \\\em \pf
 {\CC Ht An} $\eta=1/\xi$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \[

\]

 {\CC SI } $\xi=(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3})$  {\CC 5D 7V 2< ?I V*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\mu{_\eta}(t)=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\frac{\frac{1}{t}-r_{1}}{r_{2}-r_{1}},&&r_{1}\leq\frac{1}{t}<r_{2}\\
&\frac{r_{3}-\frac{1}{t}}{r_{3}-r_{2}},&&r_{2}\leq\frac{1}{t}<r_{3}\\
&0,&& \mbox{{\CC Fd K{\char123}}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},} \CCA $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\mu{_\eta}(t)=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\frac{r_{3}t-1}{(r_{3}-r_{2})t},&&\frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq t\leq\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1-r_{1}t}{(r_{2}-r_{1})t},&&\frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq t\leq\frac{1}{r_{1}}\\
&0,&& \mbox{{\CC Fd K{\char123}}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC 6T SZ HN Rb 5D} $r> 0$, $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< <F Kc Hg OB
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}=\Cr\{\xi\leq\frac{1}{r}\}=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&1,&& 0<r<\frac{1}{r_{3}}\\
&\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})},&& \frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1-r_{1}r}{2r(r_{2}-r_{1})},&& \frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{1}}\\
&0,&& r\geq\frac{1}{r_{1}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

 {\CC SZ JG~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\eta]$  {\CC 5D <F Kc 9{\char125} 3L Hg OB
} \begin{align*}
\E[\eta]=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\eta \leq r\}\dr\\
=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr\\ 
=&\int_{0}^{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}\dr+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})}\dr
+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{1}}}\frac{1-r_{1}r}{2r(r_{2}-r_{1})}\dr\\
=&\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{align*}

 {\CC =S OB {\char64}4 V{\char36} Cw 51} $r_{1}=0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA  JB J5 IO~{\char35},\CCA  TZ Ub VV Gi PN OB~{\char35},} \CCA $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}=\Cr\{\xi\leq\frac{1}{r}\}=\left\{

&\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})},&& \frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1}{2r_{2}r},&& r\geq \frac{1}{r_{2}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\eta]$  {\CC N*
} \begin{align*}
\E[\eta]=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\eta \leq r\}\dr\\
=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr\\
=&\int_{0}^{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}\dr+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})}\dr
+\lim_{d\rightarrow +\infty}\int_{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}^{d}\frac{1}{2r_{2}r}\dr\\
=&\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2r_{2}}(1+\lim_{d\rightarrow+\infty}\ln{dr_{2}}),
\end{align*}
 {\CC =a 9{\char123} 1m Cw FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA  6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

\begin{theorem}\label{theorem2-3}
 {\CC Ht D{\char35} PM} (\ref{ex-model--1}) {\CC VP 5D Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3},r_{4})$  {\CC GR } $r_{1}> 0$, {\CC Tr FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC N*

 {\CC TZ } $r_{1}=0$  {\CC 5D Gi ?v OB~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA

 {\CC SI } $\xi$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< ?I V*

&0,&& \mbox{{\CC Fd K{\char123}}}.
\end{aligned}

\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC 6T SZ HN Rb 5D} $r> 0$,$\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}=\Cr\{\xi\leq\frac{1}{r}\}=\left\{

&\frac{(r_{4}-2r_{3})r+1}{2r(r_{4}-r_{3})},&& \frac{1}{r_{4}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{3}}\\
&\frac{1}{2}, &&\frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1-r_{1}r}{2r(r_{2}-r_{1})}, &&\frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{1}}\\

\end{aligned}

 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\eta]$  {\CC N*
} \begin{align*}

+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}\frac{1}{2}\dr+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{1}}}\frac{1-r_{1}r}{2r(r_{2}-r_{1})}\dr\\
=&\frac{1}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{r_{4}}{r_{3}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{align*}

 {\CC =S OB {\char64}4 V{\char36} Cw 51} $r_{1}=0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA  JB J5 IO~{\char35},\CCA  TZ Ub VV Gi PN OB~{\char35},} \CCA $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*

 {\CC FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\eta]$  {\CC N*

\begin{theorem}\label{theorem2-4}
 {\CC Ht D{\char35} PM} (\ref{ex-model--1}) {\CC VP 5D Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG 6r {\char64}< D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $\mathrm{Er}(\lambda,r)$, {\CC Fd VP} $\xi\in[r_{1},r_2]$  {\CC GR } $r_{1}>0$, $r$  {\CC JG R; 8v U{\char125} U{\char123} J{\char125}~{\char35},} \CCA $\lambda >0$, {\CC TrSP
} \\
(1)  {\CC Ht } $r=1$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \[
\E[\eta]=\frac{e}{2\lambda}\bigg[\ln\frac{\lambda^2}{r_1r_2}+\sum_{i=1}^{+\infty}\frac{2(-1)^i-\Big(-\frac{r_1}{\lambda}\Big)^i-\Big(-\frac{r_2}{\lambda}\Big)^i}{i\cdot i!}\bigg]
+\frac{1}{\lambda}-\frac{1}{r_2},
\]
(2)  {\CC Ht } $r>1$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \begin{align*}
\E[\eta]&=\frac{e^r}{2\lambda}\Big(\frac{1}{r}\Big)^r\bigg[\Big(\frac{r_1}{\lambda}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{r_1}{\lambda}}
+\Big(\frac{r_2}{\lambda}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{r_2}{\lambda}}-2r^{r-2}e^{-r}\\
&+(r-2)\Big(\int_{\frac{r_2}{\lambda}}^{r}t^{r-3}e^{-t}\dt-\int_{r}^{\frac{r_1}{\lambda}}t^{r-3}e^{-t}\dt\Big)\bigg]+\frac{1}{\lambda r}-\frac{1}{r_2}.
\end{align*}
 {\CC TZ } $r_{1}=0$  {\CC 5D Gi ?v OB~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[1/\xi]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA
} \\\em \pf
 {\CC Ht Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG R; 8v 6r {\char64}< D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $\mathrm{Er}(\lambda,r)$, {\CC Tr } $\eta=1/\xi$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \[
\mu{_\eta}(t)=\Pos\{{\eta=t}\}=\Pos\left\{{\xi=\frac{1}{t}}\right\}=\mu{_{\xi}}\left(\frac{1}{t}\right).
\]

 {\CC SI SZ
} $$
\mu_{\xi}(t)=\left(\frac{t}{\lambda r}\right)^{r}\exp\left(r-\frac{t}{\lambda}\right),
$$
 {\CC Tr
} $$
\mu_{\eta}(t)=\left(\frac{1}{\lambda rt}\right)^{r}\exp\left(r-\frac{1}{\lambda t}\right).
$$
 {\CC Ph Gs 1d A? 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \geq x\}=\Cr\{\xi\leq\frac{1}{x}\}=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&1-\frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{1}{\lambda rx}\right)^{r}\exp\left(r-\frac{1}{\lambda x}\right),&& 0< x< \frac{1}{\lambda r}\\
&\frac{1}{2}\left(\frac{1}{\lambda rx}\right)^{r}\exp\left(r-\frac{1}{\lambda x}\right),&& \frac{1}{\lambda r}\leq x\leq \frac{1}{r_{1}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}
 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\eta]$  {\CC N*
} \begin{align*}
\E[\eta]=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq x\}\dx-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\eta \leq x\}\dx\\
=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq x\}\dx\\
=&\int_{\frac{1}{r_2}}^{\frac{1}{\lambda r}}\bigg[1-\frac{1}{2}\Big(\frac{1}{\lambda rx}\Big)^{r}e^{r-\frac{1}{\lambda x}}\bigg]\dx
+\int_{\frac{1}{\lambda r}}^{\frac{1}{r_{1}}}\frac{1}{2}\Big(\frac{1}{\lambda rx}\Big)^{r}e^{r-\frac{1}{\lambda x}}\dx,
\end{align*}
 {\CC Ht } $r=1$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \[
m=\frac{e}{2\lambda}\bigg[\ln\frac{\lambda^2}{r_1r_2}+\sum_{i=1}^{+\infty}\frac{2(-1)^i-\Big(-\frac{r_1}{\lambda}\Big)^i-\Big(-\frac{r_2}{\lambda}\Big)^i}{i\cdot i!}\bigg]
+\frac{1}{\lambda}-\frac{1}{r_2},
\]
 {\CC Ht } $r>1$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \begin{align*}
m&=\frac{e^r}{2\lambda}\Big(\frac{1}{r}\Big)^r\bigg[\Big(\frac{r_1}{\lambda}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{r_1}{\lambda}}
+\Big(\frac{r_2}{\lambda}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{r_2}{\lambda}}-2r^{r-2}e^{-r}\\
&+(r-2)\Big(\int_{\frac{r_2}{\lambda}}^{r}t^{r-3}e^{-t}\dt-\int_{r}^{\frac{r_1}{\lambda}}t^{r-3}e^{-t}\dt\Big)\bigg]+\frac{1}{\lambda r}-\frac{1}{r_2}.
\end{align*}

 {\CC =S OB {\char64}4 5D V{\char36} Cw 9{\char125} 3L Sk 6( {\char64}m} \ref{theorem2-2} {\CC :M 6( {\char64}m} \ref{theorem2-3} {\CC 5D V{\char36} Cw {\char64}` KF~{\char35},\CCA  Ub {\char64}o >M 2; TY W8 Jv~{\char35}.\CCA  6( {\char64}m V{\char36} CwMj
 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

{\bf  {\CC <G :E~{\char35}:}\CCAS }\\
$\textbf{a}=[a_{1}, a_{2},\cdots, a_{n}]$: {\CC 5{\char37} N; ?b 4f 2z F7 5D 6) 9: 3I 1>~{\char35};} \CCA \\

\subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 5D PT VJ}}
\label{pg:3.3.1} \hskip\parindent 
 {\CC <G Ph Gs Or A? N*} $\bm{\xi}=(\xi_{1},\xi_{2},\cdots,\xi_{n})$, 
 {\CC 2{\char34} <Y 6( Ph Gs} $\xi_i$, $i=1,2,\ldots,n$  {\CC JG O` ;{\char37} 6{\char64} A{\char34} 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} \cite{LiuGao2007}, {\CC Tr A* :O ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2<} $\mu_{\bm{\xi}}$  {\CC 1m J> N*
} $$

 {\CC SI SZ} $\pi_{i}(x_i,\xi_{i})$  {\CC JG 9X SZ} $\xi_i$  {\CC 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} {\char64}{\char123} Hs :/ J{\char125}~{\char35},\CCA  Tr} $\pi_{i}(x_i,\xi_{i}),i=1,2,\ldots,n$  {\CC R2 JG O` ;{\char37} 6{\char64} A{\char34} 5D~{\char35}.\CCA
 8y >] FZ M{\char123} Kc WS 5D 6{\char64} A{\char34} O{\char95} PT} \cite{Liu2003}  {\CC ?I V* FZ M{\char123} {\char64}{\char123} Hs :/ J{\char125} N*
} \[

 {\CC 2{\char34} GR 7V {\char64}k =a 9{\char123} RQ TZ 5Z 6{\char126} UB VP 8x 3v~{\char35},\CCA  Hg OB Ky J>~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
\E\Big[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})\Big]=\sum_{i=1}^{n}\bigg(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg).
\]

 {\CC =x R; 2= Tr SP
} \begin{equation*}\label{equation 1}
\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)=\E\Big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)-\E\big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\big]\Big]^{-}
=\E\Bigg[-\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)\Bigg]^{-}.
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 6T HN Rb 5D SP SP O{\char94} FZ M{\char123} V5 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $\xi_{i}$, {\CC 51 } $b_{i}\in\R, i=1,2,\ldots,n$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  SP Hg OB =a B[~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{theorem3-2}
 {\CC Ht } $\xi_{i}$  {\CC JG O` ;{\char37} 6{\char64} A{\char34} 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A? GR} $b_{i}\in\R, i=1,2,\ldots,n$, {\CC Tr SP} \\
(1)  {\CC 51 } $b_{i}\geq 0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  5H <[ 1m 4o N*
} \[
\E\Bigg[b_{i}\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)\Bigg]^{-}=b_{i}\E\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)^{-},
\]
(2)  {\CC 51 } $b_{i}< 0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  5H <[ 1m 4o N*
} \[
\E\Bigg[b_{i}\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)\Bigg]^{-}=(-b_{i})\E\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)^{+}.
\]
\\ \em \pf
 {\CC 51} $b_{i}\geq 0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  =a 9{\char123} OT H; 3I A{\char34}~{\char35}.\CCA  }

 {\CC 51 } $b_{i}< 0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  Tr SP
} \[
\E\Bigg[b_{i}\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)\Bigg]^{-} =\E\Bigg[b_{i}\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)^{-}\Bigg]
=(-b_{i})\E\bigg(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-\E\Big[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\Big]\bigg)^{+}.
\]

 {\CC 6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

\subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC T- NJ Lb 5D 5H <[ NJ Lb}}

 {\CC TZ Ub R; WS =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  N* AK D{\char35} PM 5D <F Kc :M 7V Nv~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG =+ T- NJ Lb}~(\ref{model-3-1-1})-(\ref{model-3-3-1})  {\CC W* ;/ N* Fd 5H <[ NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC ;y SZ 6( {\char64}m}~\ref{theorem3-2}, {\CC 51 } $b_{i}< 0, i=1,2,\cdots,n$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  SP Hg OB 9+ J= 3I A{\char34}

\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC 3{\char35} <{\char123} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 5D <F Kc
} \label{pg:3.4}}\hskip\parindent

 {\CC TZ Ub R; =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  =+ 4{\char38} {\char64}m} $\E\Big[\big(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-m_{i}\big)^{+}\Big],(i=1,2,\ldots,n)$  {\CC TZ H{\char125} =G~{\char35},\CCA  L] PN :M 6r {\char64}< D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D 5H <[ PN J=~{\char35}.\CCA
} \subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n}} 
\label{pg:3.4.1} \hskip\parindent 

 {\CC JW OH~{\char35},\CCA  Ub R; P{\char33} =Z LV B[ TZ H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D O` 9X =a B[~{\char35},\CCA  Hg OB Ky J>~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{theorem3-3}
 {\CC Ht Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC N* H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3})$,$r_{1}> 0$  {\CC GR } $m=\E[1/\xi]$, {\CC Tr >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{\xi}-m)^{+}\right]$  {\CC 5H <[ SZ
} \begin{align}\label{equation3-22}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{\xi}-m)^{+}\right]=&\nonumber
\begin{cases}
\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln \frac{1}{r_{2}m}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln \frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}+\frac{m(2r_{2}-r_{3})-1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})},& \frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq m<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln \frac{1}{r_{1}m}+\frac{mr_{1}-1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})},& \frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq m<\frac{1}{r_{1}}.
\end{cases}
\end{align}
 {\CC 51 } $r_{1}=0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{\xi}-m)^{+}\right]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA
} \\\em \pf
 {\CC Ht <G} $\eta=1/\xi$, {\CC Tr } $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \[
\mu{_\eta}(t)=\Pos\{{\eta=t}\}=\Pos\left\{{\xi=\frac{1}{t}}\right\}=\mu{_{\xi}}\left(\frac{1}{t}\right).
\]

 {\CC SI } $\xi=(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3})$  {\CC 5D 7V 2< ?I V*~{\char35},} \CCA $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}
\qquad &\mu{_\eta}(t)=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\frac{r_{3}t-1}{(r_{3}-r_{2})t},&&\frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq t\leq\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1-r_{1}t}{(r_{2}-r_{1})t},&&\frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq t\leq\frac{1}{r_{1}}\\
&0,&& \mbox{{\CC Fd K{\char123}}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

 {\CC 6T SZ HN Rb 5D} $r> 0$,$\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}\label{Formulation 3}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \leq r\}=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&0,&& 0<r<\frac{1}{r_{3}}\\
&\frac{r_{3}-\frac{1}{r}}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})},&& \frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{2r_{2}-r_{1}-\frac{1}{r}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})},&& \frac{1}{r_{2}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{1}}\\
&1,&& r\geq\frac{1}{r_{1}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

 {\CC SI SZ} $\E[\eta]=m=\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}$  {\CC RQ >- TZ 5Z 6{\char126} UB VP <F Kc 5C 3v~{\char35},\CCA  ?I V*
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{Formulation3-4}
\qquad &(\eta-m)^{+}=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&\eta-m,&& \eta \geq m\\
&0,&& \eta <m,
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},\CCA  51} $m\in[\frac{1}{r_{3}},\frac{1}{r_{2}})$ {\CC J1~{\char35},} \CCA $(\eta-m)^{+}$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} Hg OB~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
\begin{split}
\E[(\eta-m)^{+}]&\!=\!\int_{(m,+\infty)}(r-m)\d\Cr\{\eta\leq r\}\\
&\!=\!\int_{(m,\frac{1}{r_{2}})}\!(r\!-\!m)\d\frac{r_{3}\!-\!\frac{1}{r}}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}
\!+\!\int_{(\frac{1}{r_{2}},\frac{1}{r_{1}})}\!(r\!-\!m)\d\frac{2r_{2}-r_{1}\!-\!\frac{1}{r}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\\
&\!=\!\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln \!\frac{1}{r_{2}m}\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln\! \frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}\!+\!\frac{m(2r_{2}-r_{3})-1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}.
\end{split}
\]

 {\CC {\char64}` KF 5X~{\char35},\CCA  51} $m\in[\frac{1}{r_{2}},\frac{1}{r_{1}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  Tr SP
} \[
\E[(\eta-m)^{+}]=\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln \frac{1}{r_{1}m}+\frac{mr_{1}-1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}.
\]

 {\CC =S OB {\char64}4 V{\char36} Cw 51} $r_{1}=0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E[(\eta-m)^{+}]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC JB J5 IO~{\char35},\CCA  TZ} $r_{1}=0$  {\CC 5D Gi ?v OB~{\char35},} \CCA $\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{eqnarray*}\label{Formulation 5}
\qquad &\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}=\left\{
\begin{aligned}
&1, &&0<r<\frac{1}{r_{3}}\\
&\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})},&& \frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq r<\frac{1}{r_{2}}\\
&\frac{1}{2r_{2}r},&& r\geq \frac{1}{r_{2}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

 {\CC Rr 4K~{\char35},\CCA  FZ M{\char123} V5} $m$  {\CC ?I <F Kc 5C 3v N*
} \[
\begin{split}
m&=\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\eta \leq r\}\dr\\
&=\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\eta \geq r\}\dr\\
&=\int_{0}^{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}\dr+\int_{\frac{1}{r_{3}}}^{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}\frac{(r_{3}-2r_{2})r+1}{2r(r_{3}-r_{2})}\dr
+\lim_{d\rightarrow +\infty}\int_{\frac{1}{r_{2}}}^{d}\frac{1}{2r_{2}r}\dr\\
&=\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2r_{2}}(1+\lim_{d\rightarrow+\infty}\ln{dr_{2}}),
\end{split}
\]
 {\CC ?I V* FZ M{\char123} V5} $m$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35},\CCA  Ky RT >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E[(\eta-m)^{+}]$  {\CC R2 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA  6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd

\subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2< OB 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n}}

 {\CC 6T SZ L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs 7V 2<~{\char35},\CCA  SP Hg OB O` 9X =a B[~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{theorem3-4}
 {\CC Ht Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $(r_{1},r_{2},r_{3},r_{4})$,$r_{1}> 0$  {\CC GR } $m=\E[1/\xi]$, {\CC Tr >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\Big[\big(\frac{1}{\xi}-m\big)^{+}\Big]$  {\CC 5H <[ SZ

 {\CC 51 } $r_{1}= 0$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{\xi}-m)^{+}\right]$  {\CC 2; 4f TZ~{\char35}.\CCA

 {\CC 8y >]} $\xi$  {\CC 5D 7V 2<~{\char35},\CCA  SP
} \begin{eqnarray*}

 {\CC 6T SZ HN Rb 5D} $r> 0$,$\eta$  {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< N*

&1, && r\geq\frac{1}{r_{1}}.
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

 {\CC SI SZ} $m=\frac{1}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{r_{4}}{r_{3}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}$  {\CC RQ TZ 5Z 6{\char126} UB VP <F Kc 5C 3v~{\char35},\CCA   51} $m\in[\frac{1}{r_{4}},\frac{1}{r_{3}})$  {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA

 {\CC Ht Ph Gs} $\xi$  {\CC JG R; 8v 6r {\char64}< D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?} $\mathrm{Er}(\lambda,r)$, {\CC Fd VP} $\xi$  {\CC TZ } $[r_{1},r_2]$  {\CC IO 1d ;/ GR} $r_{1}>0$, $r$ {\CC JG R; 8v U{\char125} U{\char123} J{\char125}~{\char35},} \CCA $\lambda >0$,

\end{split}

 {\CC Fd VP

\begin{split}

 {\CC {\char64}` KF 5X~{\char35},\CCA  51} $m\in[\frac{1}{\lambda r},\frac{1}{r_1}]$  {\CC J1~{\char35},} \CCA $(\eta-m)^{+}$  {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*} \\

+\frac{e^r}{2\lambda}\Big(\frac{1}{r}\Big)^r\bigg[\Big(\frac{r_1}{\lambda}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{r_1}{\lambda}}\\
&-\Big(\frac{1}{\lambda m}\Big)^{r-2}e^{-\frac{1}{\lambda m}}-(r-2)\int_{(\frac{1}{\lambda m},\frac{r_1}{\lambda})}t^{r-3}e^{-t}\dt\bigg].
\end{split}
\]

 {\CC =S OB {\char64}4 5D 6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw 9{\char125} 3L Sk RT IO 6( {\char64}m {\char64}` KF~{\char35}.\CCA  6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

} \label{pg:3.6}}\hskip\parindent
 {\CC 1> UB M( 9{\char125} ?I PE PT {\char64}m B[ :M} L-S {\CC ;{\char125} 7V 7= 7( LV B[ AK D{\char35} :{\char125} ;7 >3 VP 4x SP 7g OU 5D ?b 4f NJ Lb~{\char35},\CCA  2{\char34} =( A{\char34} AK 7g OU 9f 1{\char92} 5D 6` 2z F7 ?b 4f D{\char35} PM~{\char35}.\CCA

\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC >x 6T 0k F+ 2n W< Tr OB 5D ?b 4f D{\char35} PM
} \label{pg:4.1}}\hskip\parindent
 {\CC TZ Ub R; UB~{\char35},\CCA  Uk 6T 6` 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ ?b 4f NJ Lb~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG =( A{\char34} R; {\char64}` 7g OU 9f 1{\char92} 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n D{\char35} PM~{\char35}.\CCA  N* AK 7= 1c Ch Jv NR CG 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n D{\char35}PM
~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG 2I SC RT OB 5D <G :E K5 Cw~{\char35}.} \CCA \\
{\bf  {\CC <G :E~{\char35}:}\CCAS }\\
$\textbf{a}=[a_{1}, a_{2},\cdots, a_{n}]$: {\CC 5{\char37} N; ?b 4f 2z F7 5D 6) 9: 3I 1>~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\textbf{p}=[p_{1}, p_{2},\cdots, p_{n}]$: {\CC 5{\char37} N; ?b 4f 2z F7 5D JU Rf~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\textbf{h}=[h_{1}, h_{2},\cdots, h_{n}]$: {\CC 5{\char37} N; 4{\char34} 4f 3I 1>~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\bm{\xi}=[\xi_{1}, \xi_{2},\cdots, \xi_{n}]$: {\CC ?b 4f NJ Lb VP 5D D{\char35} :{\char125} Ph Gs Or A?~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\textbf{x}=[x_{1}, x_{2},\cdots, x_{n}]$: {\CC ?b 4f NJ Lb VP 5D 6) 9: A? Or A?~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\gamma$: {\CC 7g OU 6H A? 2N J{\char125}~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$n$: {\CC ?b 4f 2z F7 5D VV {\char64}`~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\lambda$: {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 2N J{\char125}~{\char35};} \CCA \\
$\theta=(\theta_l,\theta_r)$: {\CC ?g 6H 2N J{\char125}~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC 6T SZ ?b 4f NJ Lb VP 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 7g OU W< Tr~{\char35},\CCA  SP RT OB <8 VV 7= 7( <S RT 2N ?<~{\char35}.} \CCA \\
(1) {\CC Ht RT D3 R; VV 2z F7 5D JU Rf :/ J{\char125} 5D Wn 4s >x 6T 0k F+ 2n N* D? 1j :/ J{\char125}~{\char35},\CCA  Tr D? 1j :/ J{\char125} Hg OB Ky J>~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
\rho_1=\max_{1\leq i\leq n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)=\max_{1\leq i\leq n}\E\Big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)-\E\big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\big]\Big]^{-}.
\]
(2) {\CC Ht RT D3 R; VV 2z F7 5D JU Rf :/ J{\char125} 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n V. :M N* D? 1j :/ J{\char125}~{\char35},\CCA  Tr D? 1j :/ J{\char125} Hg OB Ky J>~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
\rho_2=\sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)=\sum_{i=1}^{n}\E\Big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)-\E\big[\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\big]\Big]^{-}.
\]
(3) {\CC Ht RT U{\char123} Le JU Rf :/ J{\char125} 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n N* D? 1j :/ J{\char125}~{\char35},\CCA  Tr D? 1j :/ J{\char125} Hg OB Ky J>~{\char35}:\CCA
} \[
\rho_3=\rho^{-}\Big(\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})\Big)=\E\Big[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})-\E\big[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})\big]\Big]^{-}.
\]

 {\CC TZ Ub R; UB =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  2I SC 5Z} (2) {\CC VV >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 6H A? 7= 7(} $\sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)$ {\CC N* R; VV V8 1j {\char64}4 QP >? 6` 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ ?b 4f NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC ;y SZ >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 7g OU W< Tr~{\char35},\CCA  6` 2z F7 ?b 4f NJ Lb 5D K+ D? 1j D{\char35} PM 99 =( Hg OB~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-0}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\max \quad &\E[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]\\
\min \quad &\sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad &\textbf{x}\geq 0.\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}

 {\CC Ht >v 2{\char95} VF 6( U{\char95} TZ FZ M{\char123} 6) 9: JU Rf 5D Wn P{\char33} ?I =S J{\char92} K. F=} $r_{0}$ {\CC OB Q0 Gs 4x SP Wn P{\char33} 7g OU 5D 6) 9: 2{\char95} BT~{\char35},\CCA  NJ Lb} (\ref{model-4-0}) {\CC ?I W* ;/ N* RT OB 5{\char37}D?
 1j 7g OU Wn P{\char33} ;/ D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-1}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \E[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]\geq r_{0},\\
\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0.\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}

 {\CC Am R; 7= Cf~{\char35},\CCA  Ht >v 2{\char95} VF 6( U{\char95} Ok TZ Wn 4s ?I =S J{\char92} 7g OU} $s_{0}$  {\CC 5D K. F= OB Wn 4s ;/ FZ M{\char123} JU Rf~{\char35},\CCA  Tr NJ Lb} (\ref{model-4-0}) {\CC ?I W* ;/ N* RT OB 5{\char37} D? 1j JU Rf Wn 4s;/
 D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-2}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\max \quad & \E[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)\leq s_{0},\\
\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0.\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}

 {\CC Am Mb~{\char35},\CCA  N* AK Wn 4s ;/ 4x SP 7g OU 5D FZ M{\char123} JU Rf~{\char35},\CCA  ?b 4f NJ Lb} (\ref{model-4-0}) {\CC ?I =( A{\char34} N* OB Cf 5D 5{\char37} D? 1j 9f ;. D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-3}
\qquad &\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\max \quad & \E[\pi(\textbf{x},\bm{\xi})]-\gamma\sum_{i=1}^{n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0,\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
 {\CC Fd VP} $\gamma$  {\CC N* 9X SZ >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 5D R; 8v U{\char125} 7g OU 6H A? 2N J{\char125}~{\char35}.\CCA  2N J{\char125}} $\gamma$  {\CC Ch Jv AK 9X SZ >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 5D 7g OU 5D VX R* PT~{\char35},\CCA
 2N J{\char125}} $\gamma$  {\CC 5D V5 T= 5M >M T= JT M< 2; ?< BG 7g OU 6x Wn 4s ;/ FZ M{\char123} JU Rf~{\char35},\CCA  H; 6x 2N J{\char125}} $\gamma$  {\CC 5D V5 T= 8{\char95} >M T= Gc Or SZ Wn P{\char33} ;/ 7g OU~{\char35}.\CCA
} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC 5H <[ D{\char35} PM
} \label{pg:4.2}}\hskip\parindent
 {\CC TZ Ub R; WS =Z VP~{\char35},\CCA  N* AK D{\char35} PM 5D <F Kc :M 7V Nv~{\char35},\CCA  NR CG =+ T- NJ Lb}~(\ref{model-4-1})-(\ref{model-4-3})  {\CC W* ;/ N* Fd 5H <[ NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA}

 {\CC D{\char35} PM}~(\ref{model-4-1})  {\CC W* ;/ N* RT OB 5H <[ 5D 7g OU Wn P{\char33} ;/ D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-4}
&\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\E\bigg[\Big(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-m_{i}\Big)^{+}\bigg]\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}m_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\right)\geq r_{0},\\
\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0,\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
 {\CC Fd VP} $m_{i}=\E\left[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\right],\quad i=1,2,\ldots,n.$

 {\CC {\char64}` KF 5X~{\char35},\CCA  D{\char35} PM}~(\ref{model-4-2})  {\CC ?I W* ;/ N* RT OB 5H <[ 5D JU Rf Wn 4s ;/ D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-5}
&\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\max \quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i}-\frac{h_{i}m_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\right)\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \sum_{i=1}^{n}\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\E\bigg[\Big(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-m_{i}\Big)^{+}\bigg]\leq s_{0},\\
\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0,\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
 {\CC D{\char35} PM}~(\ref{model-4-3})  {\CC ?I W* ;/ N* RT OB 5H <[ 5D 7g OU JU Rf D{\char35} PM~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{eqnarray}\label{model-4-6}
&\left\{
\begin{aligned}
\max \quad &\sum_{i=1}^{n}(p_{i}x_{i}-a_{i})-\sum_{i=1}^{n}\frac{h_{i}{x_{i}^{2}}}{2}\Bigg[m_{i}+\gamma\E\bigg[\Big(\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}-m_{i}\Big)^{+}\bigg]\Bigg]\\
{\rm s.\; t.}\quad & \textbf{x}\geq 0,\\
\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray}
\noindent
 {\CC Fd VP} $m_{i}=\E\left[\frac{1}{\xi_{i}}\right],\quad i=1,2,\ldots,n.$

\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A? 5D PT VJ
} \label{pg:4.3}}\hskip\parindent
 {\CC 7V Nv IO =Z VP 5D D{\char35} PM ?I V*~{\char35},\CCA  Gs =b D{\char35} PM 5D 9X <{\char124} TZ SZ Ph Gs 59 J{\char125} 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 :M >x 6T 0k F+ 2n V5 5D <F Kc~{\char35},\CCA
 Ub R; =Z NR CG =+ LV B[ Q{\char33} Tq 1d A? 5D R; P) PT VJ <0 3{\char35} <{\char123} 2N J{\char125} ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< OB Ph Gs 59 J{\char125} FZ M{\char123} V5 :M >x 6T 0k F+ 2n V5 5D <F Kc NJ Lb~{\char35}.\CCA
} \subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC 3{\char35} <{\char123} 2N J{\char125} ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< OB 5D FZ M{\char123} V5}} 
\label{pg:4.3.1} \hskip\parindent 
 {\CC JW OH <F Kc 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A? 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A? 5D FZ M{\char123} V5~{\char35}.\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{Theorem4.1}
 {\CC <Y Ih} $\xi=[r_1,r_2,r_3;\theta_l,\theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},} \CCA $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
 Tr} $\lambda$ {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \begin{equation}\label{equation4-1}
\begin{split}
\E[\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}]=&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{4r_{2}r_{3}}{(r_{2}+r_{3})^{2}}}
+\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}\\
&+\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{split}
\end{equation}
\\\em \pf
 {\CC SI SZ} $\xi=[r_1,r_2,r_3;\theta_l,\theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},} \CCA $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
 <G ?g 6H 2N J{\char125}} $\theta=(\theta_l,\theta_r)$, {\CC Tr} $\lambda$ {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D 2N J{\char125} ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{equation*}
\mu_{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}}(x; \theta)=\left\{
\begin{array}{ll}
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](r_3-\frac{1}{x})}{r_3-r_2} , &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq x\leq\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l-1]\frac{1}{x}+[(1-\lambda)\theta_l-\lambda\theta_r]r_2+r_3}{r_3-r_2} , &\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}}< x\leq\frac{1}{r_{2}}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_r+(1-\lambda)\theta_l]\frac{1}{x}+[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l]r_2-r_1}{r_2-r_1} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_{2}}< x\leq\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](\frac{1}{x}-r_1)}{r_2-r_1} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}< x\leq\frac{1}{r_{1}}$}.\\[.2cm]
\end{array}\right.
\end{equation*}

 {\CC M( 9{\char125} <F Kc ?I V*} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< :/ J{\char125} N* Hg OB PN J=
} \begin{equation*}
\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\geq x\}=\left\{
\begin{array}{ll}
1,  &\mbox{ $0< x\leq \frac{1}{r_{3}}$}\\[.2cm]
1-\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](r_3-\frac{1}{x})}{2(r_3-r_2)} , &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_{3}}\leq x\leq\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}}$}\\[.2cm]
1-\frac{[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l-1]\frac{1}{x}+[(1-\lambda)\theta_l-\lambda\theta_r]r_2+r_3}{2(r_3-r_2)} , &\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}}< x\leq\frac{1}{r_{2}}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_r+(1-\lambda)\theta_l]\frac{1}{x}+[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l]r_2-r_1}{2(r_2-r_1)} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_{2}}< x\leq\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](\frac{1}{x}-r_1)}{2(r_2-r_1)} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}< x\leq\frac{1}{r_{1}}$}\\[.2cm]
0, &\mbox{ $ x>\frac{1}{r_{1}}$}.\\[.2cm]
\end{array}\right.
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 8y >] FZ M{\char123} V5 5D 6( Re~{\char35},\CCA  ?I 5C
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{split}
\E[\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}]=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\geq x\}\dr-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\leq x\}\dr\\
=&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{4r_{2}r_{3}}{(r_{2}+r_{3})^{2}}}
+\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}\\
&+\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{r_{3}}{r_{2}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{split}
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

 {\CC 6T SZ 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A? 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 SP Hg OB PT VJ~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{Theorem4.2}
 {\CC <Y Ih} $\xi=[r_{1}, r_{2}, r_{3}, r_{4}; \theta_l, \theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
 Tr} $\lambda$ {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D FZ M{\char123} V5 N*
} \begin{equation}\label{equation4-2}
\begin{split}
\E[\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}]=&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{4r_{3}r_{4}}{(r_{3}+r_{4})^{2}}}
+\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}\\
&+\frac{1}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{r_{4}}{r_{3}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{split}
\end{equation}
\\\em \pf
 {\CC <Y Ih} $\xi=[r_{1}, r_{2}, r_{3}, r_{4}; \theta_l, \theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 L] PN D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
 <G ?g 6H 2N J{\char125}} $\theta=(\theta_l,\theta_r)$, {\CC Tr} $\lambda$ {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D 2N J{\char125} ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< N*
} \begin{equation*} 
\mu_{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}}(x; \theta)=\left\{
\begin{array}{ll}
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](r_4-\frac{1}{x})}{r_4-r_3} , &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_4}\leq x \leq \frac{2}{r_3+r_4}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l-1]\frac{1}{x}+[(1-\lambda)\theta_l-\lambda\theta_r]r_3+r_4}{r_4-r_3} , &\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_3+r_4}< x \leq \frac{1}{r_3}$}\\[.2cm]
1, &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_3}< x \leq \frac{1}{r_2}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_r+(1-\lambda)\theta_l]\frac{1}{x}+[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l]r_2-r_1}{r_2-r_1} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_2}< x \leq \frac{2}{r_1+r_2}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](\frac{1}{x}-r_1)}{r_2-r_1} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_1+r_2} < x \leq \frac{1}{r_1}$}.\\[.2cm]
\end{array}\right.
\end{equation*}

 {\CC M( 9{\char125} <F Kc ?I V*} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D ?I PE PT 7V 2< :/ J{\char125} N* Hg OB PN J=
} \begin{equation*} 
\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\geq x\}=\left\{
\begin{array}{ll}
1, &\mbox{ $0< x \leq \frac{1}{r_4}$}\\[.2cm]
1-\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](r_4-\frac{1}{x})}{2(r_4-r_3)} , &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_4}\leq x \leq \frac{2}{r_3+r_4}$}\\[.2cm]
1-\frac{[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l-1]\frac{1}{x}+[(1-\lambda)\theta_l-\lambda\theta_r]r_3+r_4}{2(r_4-r_3)} , &\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_3+r_4}< x \leq \frac{1}{r_3}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{1}{2}, &\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_3}< x \leq \frac{1}{r_2}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_r+(1-\lambda)\theta_l]\frac{1}{x}+[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l]r_2-r_1}{2(r_2-r_1)} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{1}{r_2}< x \leq \frac{2}{r_1+r_2}$}\\[.2cm]
\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](\frac{1}{x}-r_1)}{2(r_2-r_1)} ,&\mbox{ $\frac{2}{r_1+r_2} < x \leq \frac{1}{r_1}$}\\[.2cm]
0, &\mbox{ $ x>\frac{1}{r_{1}}$}.\\[.2cm]
\end{array}\right.
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 8y >] FZ M{\char123} V5 5D 6( Re~{\char35},\CCA  ?I 5C
} \begin{equation*}\label{equation4-2}
\begin{split}
\E[\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}]=&\int_{0}^{+\infty}\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\geq x\}\dr-\int_{-\infty}^{0}\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\leq x\}\dr\\
=&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{4r_{3}r_{4}}{(r_{3}+r_{4})^{2}}}
+\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}\\
&+\frac{1}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{r_{4}}{r_{3}}}+\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}.
\end{split}
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

\subsection{\XIAOJIEZI\zihao{-4}\!\!\! {\CC 3{\char35} <{\char123} 2N J{\char125} ?I D{\char92} PT 7V 2< OB 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n}} 
\label{pg:4.3.2} \hskip\parindent 
 {\CC 6T SZ 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A? 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n~{\char35},\CCA  SP Hg OB =a B[~{\char35}:\CCA
} \begin{theorem}\label{Theorem4.3}
 {\CC <Y Ih} $\xi=[r_1,r_2,r_3;\theta_l,\theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},} \CCA $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA
 <G FZ M{\char123} V5} $\E[\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}]$ {\CC N*} $m$, {\CC Tr} $\lambda$ {\CC Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?} $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC 5D 59 J{\char125}} $\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}$ {\CC 5D >x 6T 0k F+ 2n N*} \\
(1) {\CC 51} $m\in[\frac{1}{r_{3}},\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{4r_{2}}{m(r_{2}+r_{3})^{2}}}
\!+\!\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}
\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}\ln{\frac{1}{r_{2}m}}\\
&\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}\!+\!\frac{[\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}](r_3m-1)+(r_2m-1)}{2(r_{3}-r_{2})}
-\frac{m}{2}.
\end{array}
\end{equation}
(2) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{2}{r_{2}+r_{3}},\frac{1}{r_{2}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation}

(3) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{1}{r_{2}},\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*

 {\CC SI SZ} $\xi=[r_1,r_2,r_3;\theta_l,\theta_r]$ {\CC JG 2N J{\char125} Gx <d V5 H{\char125} =G D{\char35} :{\char125} 1d A?~{\char35},} \CCA $\xi^{\lambda}$ {\CC JG} $\xi$ {\CC 5D} $\lambda$ {\CC 5D Q{\char33} Tq 1d A?~{\char35},\CCA

\end{equation}

 {\CC 8y >] >x 6T 0k F+ 2n 5D <F Kc 9+ J= ?I 5C >x 6T 0k F+ 2n N*} \\
(1) {\CC 51} $m\in[\frac{1}{r_{4}},\frac{2}{r_{3}+r_{4}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation}\label{equation--2}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]&\!=\!\int_{(m,+\infty)} (x\!-\!m) \d\Cr\{\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}\leq x\} \\
&\!=\!\int_{(m,\frac{2}{r_{3}+r_{4}})} (x\!-\!m) \d\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](r_4-\frac{1}{x})}{2(r_4-r_3)} \\
&\!+\!\int_{(\frac{2}{r_{3}+r_{4}},\frac{1}{r_3})} (x\!-\!m) \d\frac{[\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l-1]\frac{1}{x}\!+\![(1-\lambda)\theta_l-\lambda\theta_r]r_3+r_4}{2(r_4-r_3)}\\
&\!+\!\int_{(\frac{1}{r_2},\frac{2}{r_1+r_2})} (x\!-\!m) \d\Big(1\!-\!\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_r+(1-\lambda)\theta_l]\frac{1}{x}\!+\![\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l]r_2-r_1}{2(r_2-r_1)}\Big) \\
&\!+\!\int_{(\frac{2}{r_1+r_2},\frac{1}{r_1})} (x\!-\!m) \d\Big(1\!-\!\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_r-(1-\lambda)\theta_l](\frac{1}{x}-r_1)}{2(r_2-r_1)}\Big),
\end{array}
\end{equation}
 {\CC SI 9+ J=}~(\ref{equation--2}) {\CC ?I 5C
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}-(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{4r_{3}}{m(r_{3}+r_{4})^{2}}}
\!+\!\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}
\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{1}{r_{3}m}}\\
&\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}\!+\!\frac{[\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}](r_4m-1)+(r_3m-1)}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}
-\frac{m}{2}.
\end{array}
\end{equation*}


 {\CC M, {\char64}m ?I SP RT OB <F Kc =a 9{\char123}~{\char35}:} \CCA \\
(2) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{2}{r_{3}+r_{4}},\frac{1}{r_{3}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!&\frac{1-\lambda\theta_{r}+(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\ln{\frac{1}{r_3m}}
\!+\!\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}\\
&\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}\!+\!\frac{[1-\lambda\theta_{r}\!+\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}](r_3m-1)}{2(r_{4}-r_{3})}\!-\!\frac{m}{2}.
\end{array}
\end{equation*}
(3) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{1}{r_{3}},\frac{1}{r_{2}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}r_{2}}}
\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{r_{2}}{r_{1}}}\!-\!\frac{m}{2}.
\end{array}
\end{equation*}
(4) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{1}{r_{2}},\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!&\frac{\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{m(r_{1}+r_{2})^{2}}{4r_{1}}}
\!+\!\frac{1}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{1}{r_{1}m}}\\
&-\frac{[\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}](r_2m-1)-(r_1m-1)}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}.
\end{array}
\end{equation*}
(5) {\CC 51} $m\in(\frac{2}{r_{1}+r_{2}},\frac{1}{r_{1}}]$ {\CC J1~{\char35},\CCA  >x 6T 0k F+ 2n} $\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]$ {\CC N*
} \begin{equation*}
\begin{array}{ll}
\E\left[(\frac{1}{{\xi}^{\lambda}}-m)^{+}\right]\!=\!\frac{1+\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}\ln{\frac{1}{r_{1}m}}
+\frac{[1+\lambda\theta_{r}\!-\!(1-\lambda)\theta_{l}](r_1m-1)}{2(r_{2}-r_{1})}.
\end{array}
\end{equation*}

 {\CC 6( {\char64}m V{\char36} Cw Mj 1O~{\char35}.\CCA
} \pfd
\end{theorem}

\section{\JIEZI\zihao{4}\!\!\! {\CC B[ ND 5D Vw R* 9{\char36} Ww <0 44 PB 5c}}\label{pg:5.1}

 {\CC TZ QP >? D{\char35} :{\char125} ;7 >3 OB 7g OU 9f 1{\char92} 5D 6` 2z F7 5{\char37} V{\char92} FZ NJ Lb VP~{\char35},\CCA  1> B[ ND TZ 5Z H{\char125} UB :M 5Z KD UB VP 7V 1p 2I SC AK} $\max_{1\leq i\leq n}\rho^{-}\Big(\pi_i(x_i,\xi_i)\Big)$ {\CC :M

\end{aligned}
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}

\begin{itemize}
